***кучер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>ку́чер</a> (10500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kutscher</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>ку́чер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúčer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>ку́чера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>кучера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кучер.html>кучеро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>coachman <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who drives a coach</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***кушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a> (4168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въкѹшати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭkušati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kušati</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌺𐌰𐌿𐍃𐌾𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kausjan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to taste, to sample</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покушать.html>поку́шать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скушать.html>ску́шать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a guest, woman or child</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat, to have <i>(a meal)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Traditionally the word <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a></span> is used in polite invitations to eat when speaking to a woman, a child or especially to a guest. For other occasions the word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used. In colloquial speech, however, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:кушать.html>ку́шать</a> is often used instead of <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́кушать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výkušatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">доку́шать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dokúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наку́шаться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakúšatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обку́шаться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obkúšatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:откушать.html>отку́шать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otkúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***кушетка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кушетка.html>куше́тка</a> (9820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">couchette</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушетка.html>куше́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kušétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушетка.html>куше́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушетка.html>куше́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кушетка.html>куше́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>couch</li>
<li>A small sofa with no back</li></ol>

***куща.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́ща</a> (22668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kušta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kǫťa</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form still found in dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́ща</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúšča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́щи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́щи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́щ</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́щей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foliage, thicket</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tent, hut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:праздник.html>пра́здник</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:куща.html>ку́щей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prázdnik <b>kúščej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Feast_of_Tabernacles" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Feast of Tabernacles">Feast of Tabernacles</a></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="поэтическое"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатёр</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хижина.html>хи́жина</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:жилище.html>жили́ще</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Быва̀ло, прѐжних лѐт геро̀й, Око̀нчив сла̀вну бра̀нь <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> протѝвной сто̀роно̀й, Повѐсит мѐч войны̀ <a href = vnd.unilang:средь.html>средь</a> о̀тческѝя <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ку̀щи</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> тра̀гик на̀ш Буру̀н, сконча̀в чернѝльный бо̀й, Повѐсил у̀ши. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лавировать.html>лави́ровать</a> (19801)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавировать.html>лави́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lavírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tack <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to turn the bow through the wind</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вка</a> (3030)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lavà</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lávka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вок</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lávka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) bench; (small) shop/store, kiosk</li>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ной</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лавочка.html>ла́вочке</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po pʹjánoj <b>lávočke</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">when drunk, while being pissed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавра.html>лавр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lavr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лавра.html>лавр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lavr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>ла́герь</a> (912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Later borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lager</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">camp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>ла́герь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lágerʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>ла́геря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>лагеря́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лагерь.html>лагере́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>camp, camp-out</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лад</a> (23636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ladъ</i>, of unknown origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>ла́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лады́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лад.html>ладо́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́дан</a> (17115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ладанъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ladanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάδανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ládanon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́дан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ládan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́дана</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́даны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́данов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>labdanum, frankincense (a perfume often used in the rites of various religions)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дышать.html>дыша́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́дан</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dyšátʹ na ládan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be at death's door, have one foot in the grave, be in one's last days</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> чёрт <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладан.html>ла́дана</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bežátʹ, kak čórt ot ládana</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shun</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ладить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a> (14072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lad</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harmony, concord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">láditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поладить.html>пола́дить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наладить.html>нала́дить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get on <i>(with)</i>, to agree <i>(with)</i>, to be on good terms <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дят</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní ne <b>ládjat</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">they don't get on; they are at odds</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare, to make ready, to fix, to tune</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plan
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>ládil</b> v górod jéxatʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he planned to go to town</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to repeat, to keep saying, to drone <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>láditʹ</b> odnó i to že</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">harp on the same string</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладиться.html>ла́диться</a> (25356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладиться.html>ла́диться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">láditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уладиться.html>ула́диться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наладиться.html>нала́диться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work well, to advance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладиться.html>ла́дятся</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá delá ne <b>ládjatsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Things <b>are</b>n't <b>working well</b> for me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ладиться.html>ла́дилось</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó <b>ládilosʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Everything <b>was working well.</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***ладный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладный.html>ла́дный</a> (12070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладный.html>ла́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ládnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> well-built, well-formed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> comfortable, fitting nicely</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
